<Time>1619621784911< /Time><Review>Had so much fun exploring Santa Ynez. Have to admit was a bit terrified after reading about the ticks and the Poison Oak, but it turned out not to be such a big deal for us. There is definitely tons of poison oak around, didn't see any ticks (thank heavens). Just be sure to were long socks and maybe some hiking boots to protect your feet from anything. We tucked our pants in our boots and made sure to wear mosquito/tick repellent for our hike. The hike itself is so nice, not steep other than a few times and there is some minor climbing involved but definitely doable for most age groups! There's no waterfall at the moment,, probably hasn't been in a few years due to the lack of water in the "river" itself. But the hike is very green and there is a lot of shade thanks to the trees and vines and other foliage, I absolutely recommend and I will be going back myself to check it out in different times of the year!< /Review>< name>

< Review>
I came up from San Diego to visit my sis and we went on this hope, first time for both of us. Easy trail, dirt and rock, very little incline. It was April when we went to everything was pretty green and lush and the weather was perfect. We hiked up to the waterfall and saw loads of salamanders in the pools, very cool. We hiked up a little further above the falls to get some awesome views of the valley. Great easy hike or stroll.< /Review>

There's two options at the entrance, a dirt trail and a paved trail. We took the dirt trail most of the way down, and then took the paved trail back up to where we started. This worked out great for us, since we never doubled back, still made it back to our parking spot, and had easier terrain while going uphill. Overall, we walked about 6 miles. We had some great views and plenty of selfie-worthy vistas.< /text>

Deep Sentinel is a great, perhaps the best, home security system on the market today. Not only do we feel safer when we are at home, we also feel safe when we are away on vacation. Is it perfect? < text>
My car parked in my driveway was broken into just after Christmas 2019. I had Nest Cameras in which I was able to view the incident after the fact but unfortunately there was very little I or the police could they could do even with the footage provided. After finding and looking into Deep Sentinel I decided to purchase the system. This was one of the best investments I've ever made. This system provides a proactive solution. I don't have to wait for my home or vehicle to be broken into. The response time from the live security team is hands down the best I've seen. Having a live person monitoring my home gives me the piece of mind that is invaluable to me. Now I don't have to worry about having to monitoring my cameras all day or missing a notification because I'm busy at work. I've been so happy and impressed with this system that I recommend and had it installed in one of my company's satellite office locations and will be looking to add it to our other sites as well. I always recommend for anyone to do their homework on camera or security solutions but for the price point and the piece of mind this system provides in comparison to others you can't go wrong. I highly recommend Deep Sentinel.< /text>
